      Minority Leader Chuck Schumer (D-NY) pays tribute to Senator Lamar Alexander (R-TN), who gave his farewell speech that day. Mr. Alexander served 17 years as a senator. Senator Schumer also speaks about Senator-elect Mark Kelly (D-AZ).

    • Senator McConnell Tribute to Senator Lamar Alexandar

       December 2, 2020

      On the Senate floor, Majority Leader Mitch McConnell (R-KY) praises Senator Lamar Alexander (R-TN), who gave his farewell speech that day. Mr. Alexander served 17 years as a senator.

    • December 2, 2020

      President Trump Statement on 2020 Vote

      In a video statement produced by the White House, President Trump speaks about the election results. He reiterates his claims of massive voter fraud with mail-in ballots and vows to continue with his legal fight to challenge the outcome.

    • December 2, 2020

      White House Won't Say If President Trump Will Attend Inauguration

      White House Press Secretary Kayleigh McEnany declines to say if President Trump will attend the inauguration of Joe Biden on January 20. She also says no one at the White House has been interviewed by law enforcement about a pay-for-pardons scheme.

    • December 2, 2020

      Treasury Secretary Mnuchin and Federal Reserve Chair Powell Testify Before House Committee

      Treasury Secretary Steve Mnuchin and Federal Reserve Chair Jerome Powell testify before the House Financial Services Committee on their respective agencies' response to the coronavirus pandemic.

    • December 2, 2020

      Ceremonial Swearing-In of Senator-elect Mark Kelly in Old Senate Chamber

      Vice President Mike Pence participates in the ceremonial swearing-in of Sen. Mark Kelly (D-AZ). Sen. Kelly defeated Sen. Martha McSally (R-AZ) in November’s special election.
